 Hema Malini, the 'dream Girl' who has been ruling the hearts of audiences for decades, is still active in politics as well as acting
 unhone apni khubsuurati, abhinay, romance or chulbule mizaaj se hindi cinema par apni amit chhap chodi he
 Hema Malini's face as soon as you hear the evergreen songs like 'ya Jab Tak Hai Jaan', 'speak slowly, no one listens', 'zindagi Ek Safar Hai Suhana', 'tere face mein woh magic hai', 'tune o rangile' Comes to the fore
 dakshin bharat se aakar bollywood main jald hi pair jamaa lene vaali hema kaa filmi kariyar bulandiyon se bharaa rahaa he
 He was born on 16 October 1948 in Tamil Nadu
 unki maa kaa naam jaya chakravarti or pita kaa naam viesar chakravarti tha
 Before Hema's birth, her mother was so relaxed that she had already thought of her upcoming daughter's name as 'hema Malini'
 maa apni bitiyaa ko acchhee nartki bananaa chaahati thim
 Hema fulfilled this dream of her mother
 vah padhai main bhi kaaphi hoshiyaar thim
 History has been his favorite subject
 vah 10veen kaksha kii pariksha nahin de pain, kyonki unhen lagaataar abhinay ke prastaav mil rahe the
 Age was only fourteen years, but since then the filmmakers started knocking at Hema's door
 varsh 1981 main vah abhinayta dharmendra sang shaadi ke bandhan main bandha gayi
 Dharmendra and Hema, who became famous with the film 'sholay', have two daughters named Ayesha Deol and Ahana Deol
 maa or betiyaan kai cheritable kaarykram bhi prastut karti hai
 Dharmendra has four children from his first wife Prakash Kaur before marrying Hema
 dharmendra or hema malini naanaa-nani bhi ban chuke hai
 Their younger daughter Ahana Deol had recently given birth to a son
 hema malini kii maa jaya chakravarti tamil film-nirmaataa thim
 Hema Malini got her first opportunity in Hindi films in 'sapna Ka Saudagar' (1968)
 hema ke hero shoman raaj kapur the, jo umr ke maamle main hema se bahut bade the
 Raj Kapoor had said during that time that Hema would one day become a very big star of cinema and Hema made her prediction come true
 1970 main relies hui 'johny meraa naam' se hema malini ko gambhirtha se liya jane laga
 The film proved to be a super hit at the box office
 apane kariyar ke aarambh main hi hema ne dharmendra ke saath 'tum haseen main javaan' (1969), 'sharafat' (1969), 'nayaa jamaana' (1971) jaisi kuch filmein kin
 Although these films did not do much at the box office, the romance of the two went well on screen and off the screen
 varsh 1972 kii film 'sita or gita' main unhone do bhoomikaayen nibhaai
 The great success of this film made Hema a big heroine
 unhen 'dream girl' ke naam se pukaara jane laga
 a film of the same name was made by Hema's mother
 hema malini ke saundarya kaa jaadu kai film abhinaytaon par bhi chalaa
 Actors like Jeetendra and Sanjeev Kumar wanted to marry her, but later they made seven rounds with Dharmendra
 filmon main unhen dharmendra, rajesh khanna, jitendra or amitabh bachchan ke saath pasand kiya gaya
 It is noteworthy that in the year 2004, Hema Malini joined the Bharatiya Janata Party and started a political journey
 vah bharatnatyam, kuchipudi or odissi main unhone vidhivat prashikshan liya he or desh-videsh main kai stage sho pesh kiye hai
 Hema Malini has been nominated 11 times in the Filmfare Awards Best Actress category, but only once for Sita and Geeta
 hema apni sundarataa banaae rakhane ke liye pratidin yoga tathaa vyaayaam karti hai
 Fasting twice a week is a part of their regular life
 inamen ek din shuukravaar hota he
 Hema also loves Kanjeevaram saris, jasmine gems and lots of jewelery
 film 'bagban' main unki taazgi dekhakar amitabh bachchan ne kaha, "aaj bhi aap apni betiyon se adhik jawan lagati hai
 " varsh 1990 main hema malini ne chote parde kii ore bhi rukh kiya or dharawahik nupur kaa nirdesan bhi kiya
 After this, in 1992, he produced and directed the film (dil Aashna Hai) with the film actor Shah Rukh Khan
 varsh 1995 main unhone chote parde ke liye 'mohini' kaa nirmaan or nirdesan kiya
 After playing several roles in films, Hema Malini entered politics for social service and became a member of Rajya Sabha with the support of the Bharatiya Janata Party
 hema malini ko filmon main ullekhneey yogadan ke liye 1999 main filmphere kaa lifetime echishri sammaan se bhi sammanit kii gayi

 vah bhartiya janata party kii rajyasabha sadsy bhi chuni gai thim

 maa kaa shringaar unke gahanon kii chamak use anya pandalon se alag pahchaan dilaa rahi he

 The Prime Minister can ask the Chief Minister whether he was taking 1200 and 1000 rupees from the children of the rich or from the children of the poor
 ham aapako pradhanmantri kaa reva main diya gaya bayaan phir se sunaate hai
 In 2017, Anurag was watching a report by Dwari
 madhya pradesh sarkaar ne vidhansabha main sweekaar kiya tha ki rajya ke ek lakh se adhik skulon main bijli kii suvidha nahin he
 More than 50,000 teachers had vacancies
 inke bhartee kii prakriya itani jatil he ki kabhi puri nahin hoti

 eemaandaaree se dekhen to sirf shivaraj singh chouhan ke hi shashan main hi nahin, desh ke anek rajyon main har kisi ke rajya main ucch shiksha ko barbaad kiya gaya he

 madhya pradesh main sakshartaa dar he 70
 6 percent, while India averages 74 percent
 pratham sanstha kii report kahati he ki cycle baantne, scolership baantne ke baad bhi 2016 ke saal main madhya pradesh main 8
 5 percent of girls aged 11 to 14 did not attend school
 2014 main yah 6
 5 percent, Madhya Pradesh is third in the country in this case
 madhya pradesh ke skulon main hazaron kii sankhya main shikshakon ke pad lambey samay se khaali rahe hai

 bijepi ne drushti patr jari kiya he

 sabhi sarkari collejon main vyaakhyaan kakshon or sabhagaaron ko smart kakshaon main badal denge
 Experts from foreign countries will be taught through video conferencing
 tippaniyan We have not read all but is this enough? ucch shiksha ko lekar kuch thos nahin dikhaa
 Nothing is written on the resumption of teachers in the bjp's vision paper
 congress ne likhaa he ki atithi vidwaanon ko roster ke anusaar niyamit karne kii niti banaaenge
 They will not be removed in the event of non-selection from the Public Service Commission
 vigyaan mahavidhyalayon kii prayogshaalaon ko aadhunik kiya jayega
 Vyapam will be closed and selection in government services will be transparent
 skulon main shikshakon kii javabdehi sunishchit karenge
 The Board of VIII will be re-established so that the quality of education improves
 in ghoshnaptr main kya nayaa he, thos he, kya inase madhya pradesh main shiksha kaa str behatar ho sakegaa, yah vahaan ke matadaataaon ko sochna he
 It is inconceivable that even in families where people do not do education, education is not included in electoral concerns
 pradhanmantri ke mantrimandal main jayant sinha hai
 They should ask why they went to Harvard, children of some ministers are also studying abroad, they can also ask them
 shiksha ke masale ko itnaa satahi bataanaa thik nahin he
 Madhya Pradesh, which is a predominantly rural state, has so many rich people who are sending their children abroad
 bacchon ko bahes main laana thik nahin he, lekin unke hi ek kendriya mantri ne twit kiya tha ki unki beti videsh padhane ja rahi he
 People studying abroad also go on their own ability, they also go on scholarship, not only because of the richness of the rich or the rich

 We extracted the 2015-16 report from the Higher Education Department website
 jiske anusaar 28 lau college main se ek bhi lau kalege main principal nahin the
 The report for that year states that there should have been 704 professors in government colleges in Madhya Pradesh, but 474 posts were vacant
 7412 assitant professor hone chahie magar 3025 assitant professor nahin the
 a picture of government colleges of Madhya Pradesh is coming on your screen
 ye tasviren imaarat kaa baahar se andaaza detii hai magar dekh kar aap andaaza laga sakate hai ki pradhanmantri modi ke mere madhya pradesh main garibon ke bacchon ke liye kis tarah kii shiksha kaa intazaam he
 When there are no teachers, no principals, the buildings are simple and sometimes shabby, the poor will put their children there under compulsion
 use pataa he ki baahar nahin bhej saktaa, isliye kam se kam ek degree to mil jaae
 Permanent teachers were not recruited for a long time, they were replaced by the concept of guest scholars, who taught for 10 years and 15 years at a salary of less than 10,000
 atithi vidwaan sangh ke netaa ne kaha ki saal main dedh lakh kii bhi kamai nahin hui
 More than 5000 guest teachers are teaching in government colleges
 vaise shikshak sangh ke netaa madhya pradesh main isaki sankhya 12 hazaar bataate hai
 In July this year, his salary has been reduced to a minimum of 30,000, most of the visiting scholars have not received a salary of four months
 is bich sarkaar ne 3000 se adhik assitant professor kii vaikency nikaali, riselt aa gaya he magar jwining nahin hui he
 But the last stage process has been completed
 jo log paas kar chuke hai unhen pataa nahin ki chunaav ke baad niyukti patr milegaa bhi yaa nahin

 We recite to you the Prime Minister's statement in Rewa
 2017 main anuraag dwari kii ek report dekh rahaa tha
 The Madhya Pradesh government had admitted in the assembly that more than one lakh schools in the state do not have electricity
 50,000 se adhik shikshakon ke pad khaali the
 Their recruitment process is so complex that it is never completed
 aisa koi record nahin miltaa he ki ek saal ke bheetar madhya pradesh main 50,000 shikshak behaal kar liye gaye hai
 Honestly, not only under the rule of Shivraj Singh Chauhan, higher education has been ruined in everyone's state in many states of the country
 news website scrol ne pichley saal ek report likhi thi ki madhya pradesh main sakshartaa dar rashtriya ausat se kaaphi kam he
 The literacy rate in Madhya Pradesh is 70
 6 pratishat, jabaki bharat kaa ausat 74 pratishat he
 The report of the first institution says that 8 years in Madhya Pradesh in the year of 2016 even after distributing bicycles, scholarships
 5 pratishat 11 se 14 saal kii ladkiyaan skool nahin gayi
 This 6 in 2014

 Thousands of teachers' posts in schools in Madhya Pradesh have been vacant for a long time
 ab aate ki is baar vaade kya kya kiye gaye hai
 BJP has released the vision paper
 usamen shiksha ko lekar kya he dekhte hai
 Increase the gross enrollment rate in higher education institutions to 30 percent in the next five years
 2 ejineering evam 5 polytechnic collejon ko centre of excilence kii tarah unnat kiya jayega
 All government colleges will convert lecture halls and auditoriums into smart classrooms
 desh videsh ke visheshgyon se video conferencing ke madhyam se padhaayaa jayega
 The comments hamane saare to nahin padhein magar kya yah paryaapt he
 Nothing concrete was shown about higher education
 bijepi ke drushti patr main shikshakon kii bahaali par kuch nahin likhaa hua he

 lok seva ayog se chayan na hone kii sthiti main unhen nahin nikaala jayega
 The laboratories of science colleges will be modernized
 vyapam ko band kar diya jayega or shaskeey sevaaon main chayan ko pardarshi kiya jayega
 Ensure accountability of teachers in schools
 aathvin kaa board phir se sthapit kiya jayega, taaki shiksha kii gunvattta sudhare
